&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Inventories at October 31, 2018 and&#13;2017 consisted of the following:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 3 - RECENTLY ISSUED ACCOUNTING PRONOUNCEMENTS&#13;AFFECTING THE COMPANY: &lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The FASB issued&#13;ASU 2016-02, Leases (Topic 842). ASU 2016-01 requires that a lessee recognize the assets and liabilities that arise from operating&#13;leases. A lessee should recognize in the statement of financial position a liability to make lease payments (the lease liability)&#13;and a right-of-use asset representing its right to use the underlying asset for the lease term. For leases with a term of 12 months&#13;or less, a lessee is permitted to make an accounting policy election by class of underlying asset not to recognize lease assets&#13;and lease liabilities. In transition, lessees and lessors are required to recognize and measure leases at the beginning of the&#13;earliest period presented using a modified retrospective approach. Public business entities should apply the amendments in ASU&#13;2016-02 for fiscal years beginning after December 15, 2018, including interim periods within those fiscal years (i.e., January&#13;1, 2019, for a calendar year entity). Nonpublic business entities should apply the amendments for fiscal years beginning after&#13;December 15, 2019 (i.e., January 1, 2020, for a calendar year entity), and interim periods within fiscal years beginning after&#13;December 15, 2020. Early application is permitted for all public business entities and all nonpublic business entities upon issuance.&#13;The Company is currently evaluating the impact of adopting this guidance.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;In May 2014 the&#13;FASB issued ASU 2014-09, &lt;i&gt;Revenue from Contracts with Customers&lt;/i&gt;, which is a new standard related to revenue recognition.&#13;Under the new standard, recognition of revenue occurs when a customer obtains control of promised services or goods in an amount&#13;that reflects the consideration to which the entity expects to receive in exchange for those goods or services. In addition, the&#13;standard requires disclosure of the nature, amount, timing, and uncertainty of revenue and cash flows arising from customer contracts.&#13;The standard must be adopted using either a full retrospective approach for all periods presented in the period of adoption or&#13;a modified retrospective approach. In July 2015, the FASB issued ASU 2015-14, &lt;i&gt;Revenue from Contracts with Customers - Deferral&#13;of the Effective Date&lt;/i&gt;, which defers the implementation of this new standard to be effective for fiscal years beginning after&#13;December 15, 2017. Early adoption is permitted effective January 1, 2017. In March 2016, the FASB issued ASU 2016-08, &lt;i&gt;Principal&#13;versus Agent Considerations&lt;/i&gt;, which clarifies the implementation guidance on principal versus agent considerations in the new&#13;revenue recognition standard pursuant to ASU 2014-09. In April 2016, the FASB issued ASU 2016-10, &lt;i&gt;Identifying Performance Obligations&#13;and Licensing&lt;/i&gt;, and in May 2016, the FASB issued ASU 2016-12, &lt;i&gt;Narrow-Scope Improvements and Practical Expedients,&lt;/i&gt; which&#13;amend certain aspects of the new revenue recognition standard pursuant to ASU 2014-09. The Company will adopt the new standard&#13;on November 1, 2018 and currently plans to use the modified retrospective method. The majority of the Company&amp;#8217;s business&#13;is ship and bill and, on that primary revenue stream, the Company does not expect significant differences. The Company has completed&#13;its assessment of multiple arrangements and certain discount and trade promotion programs and does not expect any material adjustments.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;In July 2017, the FASB issued ASU&#13;2017-11, &amp;#8220;Earnings Per Share (Topic 260), Distinguishing Liabilities from Equity (Topic 480), Derivatives and Hedging (Topic&#13;815): I. Accounting for Certain Financial Instruments with Down Round Features, II. Replacement of the Indefinite Deferral for&#13;Mandatorily Redeemable Financial Instruments of Certain Nonpublic Entities and Certain Mandatorily Redeemable Noncontrolling Interests&#13;with a Scope Exception&amp;#8221; which addresses narrow issues identified as a result of the complexity associated with applying generally&#13;accepted accounting principles for certain financial instruments with characteristics of liabilities and equity. Part I of this&#13;Update addresses the complexity of accounting for certain financial instruments with down round features. Current accounting guidance&#13;creates cost and complexity for entities that issue financial instruments (such as warrants and convertible instruments) with down&#13;round features that require fair value measurement of the entire instrument or conversion option. Part II of this Update addresses&#13;the difficulty of navigating Topic 480, Distinguishing Liabilities from Equity, because of the existence of extensive pending content&#13;in the FASB Accounting Standards Codification. This pending content is the result of the indefinite deferral of accounting requirements&#13;about mandatorily redeemable financial instruments of certain nonpublic entities and certain mandatorily redeemable noncontrolling&#13;interests. The amendments in Part I of this Update change the classification analysis of certain equity-linked financial instruments&#13;(or embedded features) with down round features. When determining whether certain financial instruments should be classified as&#13;liabilities or equity instruments, a down round feature no longer precludes equity classification when assessing whether the instrument&#13;is indexed to an entity&amp;#8217;s own stock. The amendments also clarify existing disclosure requirements for equity-classified instruments.&#13;The amendments in Part II of this Update recharacterize the indefinite deferral of certain provisions of Topic 480 that now are&#13;presented as pending content in the Codification, to a scope exception. These amendments in Part I of this update are effective&#13;for annual and interim periods beginning after December 15, 2018, early adoption is permitted, including adoption in an interim&#13;period. If an entity early adopts the amendments in an interim period, any adjustments should be reflected as of the beginning&#13;of the fiscal year that includes that interim period. The amendments in Part I of this Update should be applied in either of the&#13;following ways: (1) Retrospectively to outstanding financial instruments with a down round feature by means of a cumulative-effect&#13;adjustment to the statement of financial position as of the beginning of the first fiscal year and interim period(s) in which the&#13;pending content that links to this paragraph is effective. (2) Retrospectively to outstanding financial instruments with a down&#13;round feature for each prior reporting period presented in accordance with the guidance on accounting changes in paragraphs 250-10-45-5&#13;through 45-10. The amendments in Part II of this Update do not require any transition guidance because those amendments do not&#13;have an accounting effect.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The FASB has&#13;issued ASU No. 2015-17, Income Taxes (Topic 740): Balance Sheet Classification of Deferred Taxes, which changes how deferred taxes&#13;are classified on organizations&amp;#8217; balance sheets. The ASU eliminates the current requirement for organizations to present&#13;deferred tax liabilities and assets as current and noncurrent in a classified balance sheet. Instead, organizations will be required&#13;to classify all deferred tax assets and liabilities as noncurrent. The amendments apply to all organizations that present a classified&#13;balance sheet. For public companies, the amendments are effective for financial statements issued for annual periods beginning&#13;after December 15, 2016, and interim periods within those annual periods. For private companies, not - for - profit organizations,&#13;and employee benefit plans, the amendments are effective for financial statements issued for annual periods beginning after December&#13;15, 2017, and interim periods within annual periods beginning after December 15, 2018. The Company adopted ASU 2015-17 during the&#13;quarter ended January 31, 2018, which did not have a material impact on its consolidated financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 8 - LINE OF CREDIT:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On April 25,&#13;2017 the Company and OPTCO (together with the Company, collectively referred to herein as the &amp;#8220;Borrowers&amp;#8221;) entered&#13;into an Amended and Restated Loan and Security Agreement (the &amp;#8220;A&amp;#38;R Loan Agreement&amp;#8221;) and Amended and Restated Loan&#13;Facility (the &amp;#8220;A&amp;#38;R Loan Facility&amp;#8221;) with Sterling National Bank (&amp;#8220;Sterling&amp;#8221;), which consolidated (i)&#13;the financing agreement between the Company and Sterling, dated February 17, 2009, as modified, (the &amp;#8220;Company Financing Agreement&amp;#8221;)&#13;and (ii) the financing agreement between Company, as guarantor, OPTCO and Sterling, dated March 10, 2015 (the &amp;#8220;OPTCO Financing&#13;Agreement&amp;#8221;), amongst other things.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Pursuant to the&#13;A&amp;#38;R Loan Agreement, the terms of each of the Company Financing Agreement and the OPTCO Financing Agreement were amended and&#13;restated to, among other things: (i) provide for a new Maturity Date of February 28, 2018; (ii) consolidate the principal amounts&#13;of the Company Financing Agreement and the OPTCO Financing Agreement to provide for a maximum principal amount limit of $12,000,000&#13;for the Borrowers, collectively, &lt;i&gt;provided that&lt;/i&gt; OPTCO is limited to a $3,000,000 maximum principal amount sublimit; (iii)&#13;expand the borrowing base to include, along with 85% of eligible accounts receivable, up to the lesser of $2,000,000 as to the&#13;Company and $1,500,000 as to OPTCO; (iv) effective March 1, 2017, converted the interest rate on the average unpaid balance of&#13;the A&amp;#38;R Loan Facility from an interest rate per annum equal to the Wall Street Journal Prime Rate to an interest rate per annum&#13;equal to the sum of the LIBOR rate plus 2.4%; (v) require the Company and OPTCO to pay, collectively, upon the occurrence of certain&#13;termination events, a prepayment premium of 1.0% (as opposed to the 0.5% under the OPTCO Financing Agreement) of the maximum amount&#13;of the A&amp;#38;R Loan Facility in effect as of the date of the termination event; (vi) eliminate the over advance fee; and (vii)&#13;establish a Letter of Credit Facility (as defined in the A&amp;#38;R Loan Agreement) with a maximum obligation amount of $1,000,000,&#13;and subject to other terms and conditions described therein. Also on April 25, 2017, SONO and CFI (collectively referred to herein&#13;as the &amp;#8220;Guarantors&amp;#8221;), entered into a Guaranty Agreement (the &amp;#8220;Guaranty Agreement&amp;#8221;) in connection with the&#13;A&amp;#38;R Loan Agreement. The Guaranty Agreement was provided as an inducement to Sterling to extend credit to Borrowers in exchange&#13;for the Guarantors&amp;#8217; unconditional guarantee of the payment and performance obligations of the Borrowers under the Loan Agreement,&#13;as further defined in the Guaranty Agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

The terms of the&#13;new agreement among other things: (i) provides for a new maturity date of March 31, 2020; (ii) increases the maximum principal&#13;amount to $14,000,000; and (iii) decreases the interest rate per annum to LIBOR plus 2 percent, 4.3% at October 31, 2018.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 5 &amp;#8211; BUSINESS ACQUISITION:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Pursuant to the terms of an Asset&#13;Purchase Agreement dated April 24, 2018 (the &amp;#8220;Generations Agreement&amp;#8221;), by and among Generations Coffee Company, LLC&#13;(&amp;#8220;GCC&amp;#8221;), the entity formed as a result of the Company&amp;#8217;s joint venture with Caruso&amp;#8217;s Coffee, Inc., Steep&#13;&amp;#38; Brew, Inc. (&amp;#8220;the Seller&amp;#8221;) a Wisconsin corporation and the stockholder of the Seller. GCC purchased substantially&#13;all the assets, including equipment, inventory, customer list and relationships (the &amp;#8220;Assets&amp;#8221;) of the Seller. This&#13;was accounted for as a business combination. GCC purchased the Assets for a purchase price consisting of $2,677,335 in cash and&#13;a Seller held promissory note for $140,510 plus assumed liabilities of $10,210. The Seller held promissory note calls for two payments&#13;of $75,000 each of principle and interest. In addition, on April 24, 2018, GCC entered into a three month advisory agreement (the&#13;&amp;#8220;Advisory Agreement&amp;#8221;), with one of the Seller&amp;#8217;s executives (the &amp;#8220;Executive&amp;#8221;), on an independent contractor&#13;basis, to ensure continuity of the business and to continue to operate the business located in Wisconsin. After completion of the&#13;first three month term, the Advisory Agreement will automatically expire, subject to renewal by mutual agreement of the parties.&#13;Pursuant to the terms of the Advisory Agreement, the Executive is entitled to cash compensation of $7,000 per month, as well as&#13;reimbursement by GCC of the Executive of up to $815 per month for health insurance benefits for the Executive paid by the seller.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company has not yet completed&#13;its full analysis of the fair value of tangible assets acquired and liabilities assumed and the allocation of any excess acquisition&#13;cost over the fair value of the net tangible net assets acquired to any separately identifiable intangible assets. Pursuant to&#13;ASC No. 805-10-25, if the initial accounting for a business combination is incomplete by the end of the reporting period in which&#13;the combination occurs, but during the allowed measurement period (which is not to exceed one year from the acquisition date),&#13;the Company retrospectively adjusts the provisional amounts recognized at the acquisition date by means of adjusting the amount&#13;recognized for goodwill.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Times

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The following pro forma results of operations&#13;for the twelve months ended October 31, 2018 and 2017 have been prepared as though the business acquisition had occurred as of&#13;October 31, 2017. This pro forma financial information is not indicative of the results of operations that the Company would have&#13;attained had the acquisition occurred at the beginning of the periods presented, nor is the pro forma financial information indicative&#13;of the results of operations that may occur in the future:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 2 - SUMMARY OF SIGNIFICANT ACCOUNTING&#13;POLICIES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;BASIS OF PRESENTATION:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The consolidated financial statements&#13;include the accounts of the Company, Organic Products Trading Company, LLC (&amp;#8220;OPTCO&amp;#8221;), Sonofresco LLC (&amp;#8220;SONO&amp;#8221;),&#13;Comfort Foods, Inc. (&amp;#8220;CFI&amp;#8221;) and Generations Coffee Company, LLC (&amp;#8220;GCC&amp;#8221;). All significant inter-company&#13;balances and transactions have been eliminated in consolidation.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;USE OF ESTIMATES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The preparation of the Company&amp;#8217;s&#13;financial statements in conformity with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America (GAAP) requires&#13;management to make estimates and assumptions that affect certain reported amounts and disclosures. Significant estimates include&#13;allowance for uncollectible accounts receivable and reserves, inventory obsolescence, depreciation, intangible asset valuations&#13;and useful lives, taxes, contingencies, and valuation of financial instruments. These estimates may be adjusted as more current&#13;information becomes available, and any adjustment could have a significant impact on recorded amounts.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;CASH:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Cash consists primarily of unrestricted&#13;cash on deposit at financial institutions and brokerage firms.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;PREPAID GREEN COFFEE:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Prepaid coffee is an item that emanates&#13;from OPTCO. The balance represents advance payments made by OPTCO to several coffee growing cooperatives for the purchase of green&#13;coffee. Interest is charged to the cooperatives for these advances. Interest earned was $6,868 and $19,430 for the years ended&#13;October 31, 2018 and 2017, respectively. The prepaid coffee balance was $0 and $171,350 as of October 31, 2018 and 2017, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;ACCOUNTS RECEIVABLE:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Trade accounts receivable are stated&#13;at the amount the Company expects to collect. The Company maintains allowances for doubtful accounts for estimated losses resulting&#13;from the inability of its customers to make required payments. Management considers the following factors when determining the&#13;collectability of specific customer accounts: customer credit-worthiness, past transaction history with the customer, current economic&#13;industry trends, and changes in customer payment terms. Past due balances over 60 days and other higher risk amounts are reviewed&#13;individually for collectability. If the financial condition of the Company&amp;#8217;s customers were to deteriorate, adversely affecting&#13;their ability to make payments, additional allowances would be required. Based on management&amp;#8217;s assessment, the Company provides&#13;for estimated uncollectible amounts through a charge to earnings and a credit to a valuation allowance. Balances that remain outstanding&#13;after the Company has used reasonable collection efforts are written off through a charge to the valuation allowance and a credit&#13;to accounts receivable.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The reserve for sales discounts represents&#13;the estimated discount that customers will take upon payment. The reserve for other allowances represents the estimated amount&#13;of returns, slotting fees and volume based discounts estimated to be incurred by the Company from its customers. The allowances&#13;are summarized as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;INVENTORIES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Inventories are stated at the lower&#13;of cost (First in, first out basis) or net realizable value, including provisions for obsolescence commensurate with known or estimated&#13;exposures. There are no reserves for obsolescence as of October 31, 2018 and 2017.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;MACHINERY AND EQUIPMENT:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Machinery and equipment are recorded&#13;at cost and depreciated using the straight-line method over the estimated useful lives of the assets. Purchases of machinery and&#13;equipment and additions and betterments which substantially extend the useful life of an asset are capitalized at cost. Expenditures&#13;which do not materially prolong the normal useful life of an asset are charged to operations as incurred. The Company also provides&#13;for amortization of leasehold improvements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;COMMODITIES HELD BY BROKER: &lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;The commodities held at broker represent&#13;the market value of the Company&amp;#8217;s trading account, which consists of option and future contracts for coffee held with a brokerage&#13;firm. The Company uses options and futures contracts, which are not designated or qualifying as hedging instruments, to partially&#13;hedge the effects of fluctuations in the price of green coffee beans. Options and futures contracts are recognized at fair value&#13;in the consolidated financial statements with current recognition of gains and losses on such positions. The Company&amp;#8217;s accounting&#13;for options and futures contracts may increase earnings volatility in any particular period.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;The Company has open position contracts&#13;held by the broker, which are summarized as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;The Company classifies its options&#13;and future contracts as trading securities and accordingly, unrealized holding gains and losses are included in earnings.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;At October 31, 2018, the Company&#13;held 22 futures contracts (generally with terms of three to four months) for the purchase of 825,000 pounds of green coffee at&#13;a weighted average price of $1.11 per pound. The fair market value of coffee applicable to such contracts was $1.13 per pound at&#13;that date. At October 31, 2018, the Company held 65 option covering an aggregate of 2,437,500 pounds of green coffee beans from&#13;$1.125 to $1.15 per pound. The fair market value of these options, which was obtained from observable market data of similar instruments&#13;was $52,594.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;At October 31, 2017, the Company&#13;held 145 futures contracts (generally with terms of three to four months) for the purchase of 5,437,500 pounds of green coffee&#13;at a weighted average price of $1.31 per pound. The fair market value of coffee applicable to such contracts was $1.25 per pound&#13;at that date. At October 31, 2017, the Company did not have any options.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;Included in cost of sales for the&#13;years ended October 31, 2018 and 2017, the Company recorded realized and unrealized gains and losses respectively, on these contracts&#13;as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;GOODWILL AND TRADEMARKS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company has determined that its&#13;goodwill and trademarks, which consist of product lines, trade names and packaging designs have an indefinite useful life. The&#13;value of the goodwill and trademarks was allocated based on an independent valuation. Goodwill and trademarks are not amortized&#13;but are assigned to a specific reporting unit or asset class and tested for impairment at least annually or upon the occurrence&#13;of an event or when circumstances indicate that the reporting unit&amp;#8217;s carrying amount of goodwill and trademarks is greater&#13;than its fair value. As of October 31, 2018 and 2017, the Company has determined by using a qualitative assessment that an impairment&#13;did not exist. In 2011, the Company adopted Financial Accounting Standard ASB ASU 2011-08 Intangibles &amp;#8211; Goodwill and Other&#13;&amp;#8211; Testing Goodwill for Impairment, which allows an entity to first assess qualitative factors to determine whether it is&#13;necessary to perform the two-step quantitative goodwill impairment test. Under this amendment, an entity would not be required&#13;to calculate the fair value of a reporting unit unless the entity determines, based on a qualitative assessment, that it is more&#13;likely than not that its fair value is less than its carrying amount. The amendment includes a number of events and circumstances&#13;for an entity to consider in conducting the qualitative assessment.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;CUSTOMER LIST AND RELATIONSHIPS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Customer list and relationships&#13;consist of a specific customer lists and customer contracts obtained by the Company in the acquisition of OPTCO, Comfort&#13;Foods, Sonofresco and Steep &amp;#38; Brew which are being amortized on the straight-line method over their estimated useful life&#13;of twenty years.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;ADVERTISING:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company expenses the cost of&#13;advertising and promotion as incurred. Advertising costs charged to operations totaled $366,665 and $243,658 for the years ended&#13;October 31, 2018 and 2017, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;INCOME TAXES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company accounts for income taxes&#13;pursuant to the asset and liability method which requires deferred income tax assets and liabilities to be computed for temporary&#13;differences between the financial statement and tax basis of assets and liabilities that will result in taxable or deductible amounts&#13;in the future based on enacted tax laws and rates applicable to the periods in which the differences are expected to affect taxable&#13;income. Valuation allowances are established when necessary to reduce deferred tax assets to the amount expected to be realized.&#13;The income tax provision or benefit is the tax incurred for the period plus or minus the change during the period in deferred tax&#13;assets and liabilities.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;EARNINGS PER SHARE:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Basic earnings per common share were&#13;computed by dividing net income by the sum of the weighted-average number of common shares outstanding. Diluted earnings per common&#13;share is computed by dividing the net income by the weighted-average number of common shares outstanding plus the dilutive effect&#13;of common shares issuable upon exercise of potential sources of dilution.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The weighted average common shares&#13;outstanding used in the computation of basic and diluted earnings per share were 5,691,057 and 5,858,376 for the years ended October&#13;31, 2018 and 2017, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;FAIR VALUE OF FINANCIAL INSTRUMENTS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The carrying amounts of cash, accounts&#13;receivable, notes receivable, accounts payable and accrued expenses approximate fair value because of the short-term nature of&#13;these instruments. The carrying amount of the bank line of credit borrowings approximates fair value because the debt is based&#13;on current rates at which the Company could borrow funds with similar remaining maturities. Fair value estimates are made at a&#13;specific point in time, based on relevant market information about the financial instruments when available. These estimates are&#13;subjective in nature and involve uncertainties and matters of significant judgment and therefore, cannot be determined with precision.&#13;Changes in assumptions could significantly affect the estimates.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;REVENUE RECOGNITION:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company recognizes revenue in&#13;accordance with the authoritative guidance. Revenue is recognized at the point title and risk of ownership transfers to its customers&#13;upon the Company&amp;#8217;s shippers taking possession of the goods at the time of shipment because i) title passes in accordance&#13;with the terms of the Company&amp;#8217;s purchase orders and with its agreements with its customers, ii) any risk of loss is covered&#13;by the Company&amp;#8217;s customers&amp;#8217; insurance, iii) there is persuasive evidence of a sales arrangement, iv) the sales price&#13;is determinable and v) collection of the resulting receivable is reasonably assured. Thus, revenue is recognized at the point of&#13;shipment to its customers.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Returns: The Company does not accept&#13;returns for damaged goods on packaged coffee and usable green coffee, as the customer takes possession of our product at the point&#13;of shipment. In the event a customer claims receipt of damaged goods, the Company, acting as an agent on behalf of the customer,&#13;may file a claim for reimbursement with the shipper. The Company is not obligated or required to act as an agent on behalf of its&#13;customers, but may make the business decision to do so as a convenience to its customers. The shipper keeps the damaged product.&#13;The Company will then ship a completely new order to the customer once a claim has been filed and the Company receives reimbursement&#13;or credit from the shipper for the initial shipment. The Company does evaluate the need, if any, of an accrual for returns for&#13;damaged goods. To date, returns for damaged goods have been immaterial. The Company estimates that, based on historical trends,&#13;that future returns for damaged goods should also be immaterial.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;In the event that the Company ships&#13;an incorrect order or has returns for short dated product, the Company will accept those two types of items back as returns. The&#13;amount for these two types of returns are estimated, accrued and recognized at the date of sale. These amounts are included in&#13;the determination of net sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Slotting fees: Certain retailers&#13;require the payment of slotting fees in order to obtain space for the Company&amp;#8217;s products on the retailer&amp;#8217;s store shelves.&#13;The cost of these fees are estimated, accrued and recognized at the earlier of the date cash is paid or a liability to the retailer&#13;is created. The amounts are included in the determination of net sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Sales discounts: The amount of sales&#13;discounts are estimated, accrued and recognized at the date of the sale. These amounts are included in the determination of net&#13;sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Volume-based incentives: These incentives&#13;typically involve rebates or refunds of a specific amount of cash consideration that are redeemable only if the reseller completes&#13;a specified cumulative level of sales transactions. Under incentive programs of this nature, the Company estimates and accrues&#13;the cost of the rebate when it is taken by the reseller. These amounts are included in the determination of net sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Cooperative advertising: Under these&#13;arrangements, the Company will agree to reimburse the reseller for a portion of the costs incurred by the reseller to advertise&#13;and promote certain of the Company&amp;#8217;s products. The Company estimates, accrues and recognizes the cost of cooperative advertising&#13;programs in the period in which the advertising and promotional activity first takes place. The costs of these incentives are included&#13;in advertising expense.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;SHIPPING AND HANDLING FEES AND&#13;COSTS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Revenue earned from shipping and&#13;handling fees is reflected in net sales. Costs associated with shipping product to customers aggregating approximately $3,144,000&#13;and $2,412,000 for the years ended October 31, 2018 and 2017, respectively, is included in selling and administrative expenses.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;CONCENTRATION OF RISK:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Financial instruments that potentially&#13;subject the Company to concentrations of credit risk consist principally of cash deposits at financial institutions and brokerage&#13;firms.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Accounts at each institution are&#13;insured by the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation (FDIC) up to certain limits. At October 31, 2018 and 2017, the Company had&#13;approximately $2,800,000 and $176,000 in excess of FDIC insured limits, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The accounts at the brokerage firm&#13;contain cash and securities. Balances are insured up to $500,000, with a limit of $100,000 for cash, by the Securities Investor&#13;Protection Corporation (SIPC). At October 31, 2018 and 2017, the Company had approximately $355,000 and $1,122,000 in excess of&#13;SIPC insured limits, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;See Note 10 for concentration of&#13;risks with respect to trade receivables and purchases from accounts payable vendors.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;OPERATING LEASES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company has operating lease agreements&#13;for its corporate office and warehouses, some of which contain provisions for future rent increases or periods in which rent payments&#13;are abated. Operating leases which provide for lease payments that vary materially from the straight-line basis are adjusted for&#13;financial accounting purposes to reflect rental income or expense on the straight-line basis in accordance with the authoritative&#13;guidance issued by the FASB. The excess of straight-line rent over actual payments by the Company of $242,143 and $240,379 is presented&#13;as deferred rent payable as of October 31, 2018 and 2017, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;RECLASSIFICATION:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Certain amounts in the prior year&#13;financial statements have been reclassified to conform to the current presentation. These reclassification adjustments had no effect&#13;on the Company&amp;#8217;s previously reported net income.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;EQUITY METHOD OF ACCOUNTING:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -1in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Investee companies that are not consolidated,&#13;but over which the Company exercises significant influence, are accounted for under the equity method of accounting. Whether or&#13;not the Company exercises significant influence with respect to an Investee depends on an evaluation of several factors including,&#13;among others, representation on the Investee company&amp;#8217;s board of directors and ownership level, which is generally a 20% to&#13;50% interest in the voting securities of the Investee company. Under the equity method of accounting, an Investee company&amp;#8217;s&#13;accounts are not reflected within the Company&amp;#8217;s Consolidated Balance Sheets and Consolidated Statements of Income; however,&#13;the Company&amp;#8217;s share of the earnings or losses of the Investee company is reflected in the caption &amp;#8220;Loss from equity&#13;method investments&amp;#8221; in the Consolidated Statements of Income. The Company&amp;#8217;s carrying value in an equity method Investee&#13;company is reflected in the caption &amp;#8220;Equity method investments&amp;#8221; in the Company&amp;#8217;s Consolidated Balance Sheets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 6 - PURCHASE OF BUSINESS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Pursuant to the terms of a Stock&#13;Purchase Agreement dated February 23, 2017, by and among the Company, Comfort Foods, Inc., a Massachusetts corporation (&amp;#8220;CFI&amp;#8221;),&#13;Stephen J. Beattie (the &amp;#8220;Trustee&amp;#8221;), as trustee of the Stephen J. Beattie Revocable Trust of 2013 (the &amp;#8220;Trust&amp;#8221;)&#13;and Victor Janovich (together, with the Trustee on behalf of the Trust, the &amp;#8220;Sellers&amp;#8221;), the Company, acquired all of&#13;the outstanding capital stock of CFI. The transaction was accounted for as a business combination and was not a significant acquisition&#13;for the Company. The purpose of the transaction was to expand the Company&amp;#8217;s presence in the northeast. The Company purchased&#13;the shares of capital stock for a purchase price of $2,300,000 in cash, subject to the holdback of $25,000 for a six month period&#13;following the consummation of the transaction to secure the Sellers&amp;#8217; indemnification obligations. In addition, immediately&#13;following consummation of the transaction, the Company also paid all of the existing bank debt of CFI, totaling approximately $605,173.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;As part of the transaction, the employees&#13;of CFI remained employees of CFI, with the exception of Stephen Beattie, CFI&amp;#8217;s then Chief Executive Officer. Mr. Beattie&#13;entered into an advisory agreement (the &amp;#8220;Advisory Agreement&amp;#8221;) with CFI, dated as of February 23, 2017, pursuant to&#13;which Mr. Beattie agreed to provide services to CFI on an independent contractor basis, to ensure continuity of the business and&#13;its operations in Massachusetts. The initial term of the Advisory Agreement commenced on April 1, 2017 and was set to expire on&#13;December 31, 2017, unless terminated earlier in accordance with the terms and conditions of the Advisory Agreement. On September&#13;6, 2017, the Company terminated the Advisory Agreement. Pursuant to the terms of the Advisory Agreement, Mr. Beattie was paid $5,000&#13;per month.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 10 - COMMITMENTS AND CONTINGENCIES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;OPERATING LEASES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;In February 2004, the Company entered&#13;into a lease for office and warehouse space in La Junta City, Colorado. This lease, which is at a monthly rental of $8,341 beginning&#13;January 2005, expires on January 31, 2024. Rent charged to operations amounted to $95,504 for the years ended October 31, 2018&#13;and 2017.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;In October 2008, the Company entered&#13;into a lease for office and warehouse space in Staten Island, NY. This lease, which is at a monthly rental beginning November 2008,&#13;expires on October 31, 2023 and includes annual rent increases. Rent charged to operations amounted to $143,171 for the years ended&#13;October 31, 2018 and 2017. The Company also uses a variety of independent, bonded commercial warehouses to store its green coffee&#13;beans.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.8in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;In March 2015, the Company entered&#13;into a lease for office space in Vancouver, WA. This lease, which is at a monthly rental beginning April 1, 2015, expired on March&#13;31, 2017. The lease was extended, effective as of April 1, 2017 and expiring on March 31, 2019. Rent charged to operations amounted&#13;to $38,943 and $37,130 for the years ended October 31, 2018 and 2017, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;In December 2016, the Company entered&#13;into a lease for office and warehouse space in Burlington, WA. This lease, which is at a monthly rental beginning December 1, 2017,&#13;expired on December 31, 2018. The lease was extended, effective January 1, 2019 and expiring on December 31, 2019. Rent charged&#13;to operations amounted to $46,190 and $43,988 for the years ended October 31, 2018 and 2017, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;In April 2017, the Company entered&#13;into a lease for office and warehouse space in North Andover, MA. This lease, which is at a monthly rental beginning April 1, 2017,&#13;expires on March 31, 2027 and includes charges for common areas and utilities. Rent charged to operations amounted to $233,750&#13;and $172,627 for the years ended October 31, 2018 and 2017, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.8in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

   &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;2,858,607&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;401 (K) RETIREMENT PLAN:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 4.5pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;NOTE 14 - FAIR VALUE MEASUREMENTS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Fair value is the price that would&#13;be received to sell an asset or paid to transfer a liability in an orderly transaction between market participants at the measurement&#13;date, not adjusted for transaction costs. The guidance also establishes a fair value hierarchy that prioritizes the inputs to valuation&#13;techniques used to measure fair value into three broad levels giving the highest priority to quoted prices in active markets for&#13;identical assets or liabilities (Level 1) and the lowest priority to unobservable inputs (Level 3) as described below:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Level 1 Inputs &amp;#8211; Unadjusted&#13;quoted prices in active markets for identical assets or liabilities that are accessible by the Company;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Level 2 Inputs &amp;#8211; Quoted prices&#13;in markets that are not active or financial instruments for which all significant inputs are observable, either directly or indirectly;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Level 3 Inputs &amp;#8211; Unobservable&#13;inputs for the asset or liability including significant assumptions of the Company and other market participants.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company determines fair values&#13;for its investment assets as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Investments at fair value consist&#13;of commodity securities and deferred compensation plan assets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company maintains a deferred&#13;compensation plan. The fair value of the plan assets are classified within Level 1 as the assets are valued using quoted prices&#13;in active markets. The assets are included with Deposits and other assets in the accompanying balance sheets. Additional information&#13;related to the Company&amp;#8217;s deferred compensation plan is disclosed in Note 11.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company&amp;#8217;s commodity securities&#13;are classified within Level 2 and include coffee futures and options contracts. To determine fair value, the Company utilizes the&#13;market approach valuation technique for the coffee futures and options contracts. The Company uses Level 2 inputs that are based&#13;on market data of similar instruments that are in observable markets. All commodities on the balance sheet are recorded at fair&#13;value with changes in fair value included in earnings.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The following tables present the&#13;Company&amp;#8217;s assets and liabilities that are measured at fair value on a recurring basis and are categorized using the fair&#13;value hierarchy.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 style=text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=10 style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fair Value Measurements as of October 31, 2018&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Total&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Level 1&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13; &lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;PREPAID GREEN COFFEE:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;ACCOUNTS RECEIVABLE:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Trade accounts receivable are stated&#13;at the amount the Company expects to collect. The Company maintains allowances for doubtful accounts for estimated losses resulting&#13;from the inability of its customers to make required payments. Management considers the following factors when determining the&#13;collectability of specific customer accounts: customer credit-worthiness, past transaction history with the customer, current economic&#13;industry trends, and changes in customer payment terms. Past due balances over 60 days and other higher risk amounts are reviewed&#13;individually for collectability. If the financial condition of the Company&amp;#8217;s customers were to deteriorate, adversely affecting&#13;their ability to make payments, additional allowances would be required. Based on management&amp;#8217;s assessment, the Company provides&#13;for estimated uncollectible amounts through a charge to earnings and a credit to a valuation allowance. Balances that remain outstanding&#13;after the Company has used reasonable collection efforts are written off through a charge to the valuation allowance and a credit&#13;to accounts receivable.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The reserve for sales discounts represents&#13;the estimated discount that customers will take upon payment. The reserve for other allowances represents the estimated amount&#13;of returns, slotting fees and volume based discounts estimated to be incurred by the Company from its customers. The allowances&#13;are summarized as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;INVENTORIES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;MACHINERY AND EQUIPMENT:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;COMMODITIES HELD BY BROKER: &lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;The commodities held at broker represent&#13;the market value of the Company&amp;#8217;s trading account, which consists of option and future contracts for coffee held with a brokerage&#13;firm. The Company uses options and futures contracts, which are not designated or qualifying as hedging instruments, to partially&#13;hedge the effects of fluctuations in the price of green coffee beans. Options and futures contracts are recognized at fair value&#13;in the consolidated financial statements with current recognition of gains and losses on such positions. The Company&amp;#8217;s accounting&#13;for options and futures contracts may increase earnings volatility in any particular period.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;The Company has open position contracts&#13;held by the broker, which are summarized as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

   &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;$&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;(22,046&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;)&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;$&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;(210,862&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;)&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;The Company classifies its options&#13;and future contracts as trading securities and accordingly, unrealized holding gains and losses are included in earnings.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;At October 31, 2018, the Company&#13;held 22 futures contracts (generally with terms of three to four months) for the purchase of 825,000 pounds of green coffee at&#13;a weighted average price of $1.11 per pound. The fair market value of coffee applicable to such contracts was $1.13 per pound at&#13;that date. At October 31, 2018, the Company held 65 option covering an aggregate of 2,437,500 pounds of green coffee beans from&#13;$1.125 to $1.15 per pound. The fair market value of these options, which was obtained from observable market data of similar instruments&#13;was $52,594.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;At October 31, 2017, the Company&#13;held 145 futures contracts (generally with terms of three to four months) for the purchase of 5,437,500 pounds of green coffee&#13;at a weighted average price of $1.31 per pound. The fair market value of coffee applicable to such contracts was $1.25 per pound&#13;at that date. At October 31, 2017, the Company did not have any options.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;Included in cost of sales for the&#13;years ended October 31, 2018 and 2017, the Company recorded realized and unrealized gains and losses respectively, on these contracts&#13;as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
