 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;GOODWILL AND TRADEMARKS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;CUSTOMER LIST AND RELATIONSHIPS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;ADVERTISING:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;INCOME TAXES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;EARNINGS PER SHARE:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Basic earnings per common share were&#13;computed by dividing net income by the sum of the weighted-average number of common shares outstanding. Diluted earnings per common&#13;share is computed by dividing the net income by the weighted-average number of common shares outstanding plus the dilutive effect&#13;of common shares issuable upon exercise of potential sources of dilution.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;FAIR VALUE OF FINANCIAL INSTRUMENTS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;REVENUE RECOGNITION:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The Company recognizes revenue in&#13;accordance with the authoritative guidance. Revenue is recognized at the point title and risk of ownership transfers to its customers&#13;upon the Company&amp;#8217;s shippers taking possession of the goods at the time of shipment because i) title passes in accordance&#13;with the terms of the Company&amp;#8217;s purchase orders and with its agreements with its customers, ii) any risk of loss is covered&#13;by the Company&amp;#8217;s customers&amp;#8217; insurance, iii) there is persuasive evidence of a sales arrangement, iv) the sales price&#13;is determinable and v) collection of the resulting receivable is reasonably assured. Thus, revenue is recognized at the point of&#13;shipment to its customers.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Returns: The Company does not accept&#13;returns for damaged goods on packaged coffee and usable green coffee, as the customer takes possession of our product at the point&#13;of shipment. In the event a customer claims receipt of damaged goods, the Company, acting as an agent on behalf of the customer,&#13;may file a claim for reimbursement with the shipper. The Company is not obligated or required to act as an agent on behalf of its&#13;customers, but may make the business decision to do so as a convenience to its customers. The shipper keeps the damaged product.&#13;The Company will then ship a completely new order to the customer once a claim has been filed and the Company receives reimbursement&#13;or credit from the shipper for the initial shipment. The Company does evaluate the need, if any, of an accrual for returns for&#13;damaged goods. To date, returns for damaged goods have been immaterial. The Company estimates that, based on historical trends,&#13;that future returns for damaged goods should also be immaterial.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;In the event that the Company ships&#13;an incorrect order or has returns for short dated product, the Company will accept those two types of items back as returns. The&#13;amount for these two types of returns are estimated, accrued and recognized at the date of sale. These amounts are included in&#13;the determination of net sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Slotting fees: Certain retailers&#13;require the payment of slotting fees in order to obtain space for the Company&amp;#8217;s products on the retailer&amp;#8217;s store shelves.&#13;The cost of these fees are estimated, accrued and recognized at the earlier of the date cash is paid or a liability to the retailer&#13;is created. The amounts are included in the determination of net sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Sales discounts: The amount of sales&#13;discounts are estimated, accrued and recognized at the date of the sale. These amounts are included in the determination of net&#13;sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Volume-based incentives: These incentives&#13;typically involve rebates or refunds of a specific amount of cash consideration that are redeemable only if the reseller completes&#13;a specified cumulative level of sales transactions. Under incentive programs of this nature, the Company estimates and accrues&#13;the cost of the rebate when it is taken by the reseller. These amounts are included in the determination of net sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;SHIPPING AND HANDLING FEES AND&#13;COSTS:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;CONCENTRATION OF RISK:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Financial instruments that potentially&#13;subject the Company to concentrations of credit risk consist principally of cash deposits at financial institutions and brokerage&#13;firms.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Accounts at each institution are&#13;insured by the Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation (FDIC) up to certain limits. At October 31, 2018 and 2017, the Company had&#13;approximately $2,800,000 and $176,000 in excess of FDIC insured limits, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;The accounts at the brokerage firm&#13;contain cash and securities. Balances are insured up to $500,000, with a limit of $100,000 for cash, by the Securities Investor&#13;Protection Corporation (SIPC). At October 31, 2018 and 2017, the Company had approximately $355,000 and $1,122,000 in excess of&#13;SIPC insured limits, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;OPERATING LEASES:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;EQUITY METHOD OF ACCOUNTING:&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 1in; text-align: justify; text-indent: -1in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 0.5in; text-align: justify&gt;Investee companies that are not consolidated,&#13;but over which the Company exercises significant influence, are accounted for under the equity method of accounting. Whether or&#13;not the Company exercises significant influence with respect to an Investee depends on an evaluation of several factors including,&#13;among others, representation on the Investee company&amp;#8217;s board of directors and ownership level, which is generally a 20% to&#13;50% interest in the voting securities of the Investee company. Under the equity method of accounting, an Investee company&amp;#8217;s&#13;accounts are not reflected within the Company&amp;#8217;s Consolidated Balance Sheets and Consolidated Statements of Income; however,&#13;the Company&amp;#8217;s share of the earnings or losses of the Investee company is reflected in the caption &amp;#8220;Loss from equity&#13;method investments&amp;#8221; in the Consolidated Statements of Income. The Company&amp;#8217;s carrying value in an equity method Investee&#13;company is reflected in the caption &amp;#8220;Equity method investments&amp;#8221; in the Company&amp;#8217;s Consolidated Balance Sheets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 38.9pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=margin: 0pt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Times
